< review>
Absolutely amazing service, we showed up as a large group, and stayed nearly till close. All the sushi provided was great quality, and they let us try many things, including a dish not on the menu. the proportions (being a person from the south east, i tend to eat a lot) where enough to fill me before i finished the entire order. The chicken heart, which I expected not to taste great, and the waitress did not try to sell to me, was excellent and something I will be on the hunt for in the future. The mochi ice cream was top quality, and I tried all of the flavors available except the mango. Ultimately my party cleaned out a lot of their stock, and there was not a single complaint from staff. They where all too happy to serve us with smiles and casual jokes.</review>

< review>
When I arrived with a large group, we were seated promptly and got to order with little wait. Immediately we were met with a cozy, casual atmosphere and friendly staff.

When our food arrived‚Äîwhich didn't take long at all‚Äîthe takoyaki was piping hot and succulent, and the spider roll was delicious. And just when I thought I was full, the black sesame mochi was a sweet, light way to finish off the night. All throughout, our hosts were more than gracious, with a few extra dishes on the house.

If I'm in the area again, I'll make it a point to return! All in all, a fantastic experience.</review>

< name>
Adam K<//name>
< Review>
Lacks the creativity, taste and texture of original concepts like Smitten, which it seeks to emulate. The ice cream itself is good, although their selection of flavors is fairly predictable and certainly doesn't warrant the price point. Beyond the "cool factor" of being immersed in a giant cloud there's no clear evidence that the liquid nitrogen necessarily produces better tasting or better quality ice cream. In fact, their consistency is a extremely dense, as opposed to creamy, which feels off to me. Would recommend just going to any other ice cream store or the grocery store instead, and saving money and time (the service is inefficient because of a confusing menu and a complex production process which can result in long lines).

< Text>
Five stars for being a legendary iconic dive bar perfect for chillin and listening to classic music with fantastic drinks, gastropub food that offers great value. The huge interior fireplace and glow of red candle globes provide perfect relief from the deliciously cool ocean breezes blowing the original French windows.  This really is perfection and the polar opposite of overly stylized modern restaurants.</Text>

< review>
I found this small but busy shop when I needed to get a friend‚Äôs tire patched and was nearby. I saw their ratings, and I figured I could not go wrong here.
Several weeks later, I brought my vehicle in to have some KW coil overs by MPP installed. I enjoyed speaking with JT, who seemed to be very passionate and caring about his work. Their price for the installation, ride height adjustment to 1 inch below stock, as well as alignment was $350, around half that of a respectable suspension shop.
I confirmed that they would be able to finish in one day ‚Äì drop off the day before, pick up the day after. It took them more time than they thought it would, so they needed it another day. OK, no problem ‚Äì I changed my plans and made alternate transportation arrangements.
When I got the vehicle back, the ride height was very low ‚Äì substantially lower than I wanted and had originally asked for. No problem, JT and his brother said ‚Äì bring it back if you still want it higher after driving it for a while. I did so a few days later, and JT raised it a small amount ‚Äì still lower than I had asked for. These are the values specified by Mountain Pass Performance for the ‚Äúmild‚Äù drop.
After JT did not feel comfortable adjusting the ride height to  manufacturer specifications, I emailed a photo of the front suspension install to the manufacturer of the coil overs to verify that the installation was properly done. They pointed out that their directions had not been followed, and that an extra rubber piece was reinstalled from the stock suspension setup that was not supposed to be there. The manufacturer was kind enough to offer to speak with JT, the mechanic who worked on the car. After some time (JT said he would call the other gentleman, who never received a phone call), the coilover manufacturer was kind enough to reach out to JT directly. They spoke for some time, but it seems as if JT did not want to take advice from ‚Äúsome guy in Canada‚Äù. (He later stated that he did not like that I was calling other people / mechanics to discuss his work ‚Äì ‚ÄúI am an ASE certified mechanic!‚Äù).
After some back and forth, JT agreed to correct the installation and said to come by today (12/8/20) at 4:00 PM for the work to be done. I asked if he would be able to finish the vehicle same day, and he said he would call back at 11:00 AM to verify, which he never did. I went by the shop at 4:15 PM, thinking that he had forgotten to call me back, but would honor his 4:00 PM appointment.
After waiting in the shop for 15 minutes, JT says he cannot to the work today ‚Äì ‚Äúlook around ‚Äì I am busy today, my helpers quit‚Äù (paraphrased). At this point, things headed south, and JT offered to refund my money. His brother stepped in at this point, and said he would not do that. After some shouting back and forth, JT and his brother ask me to leave ‚Äúgood bye ‚Äì have a nice day‚Äù is a phrase that JT likes to say. I like that phrase; I might start using it.
On initially stumbling across this place, I thought I had found a caring mechanic that I could recommend friends and family to. I now have to take my vehicle to another shop (I‚Äôm not going to cheap out this time ‚Äì in some things, you get what you pay for) to have the suspension removed and properly reinstalled, as well as have the ride height adjusted to 135mm.
Hopefully JT and I just had a personality mismatch combined with consistent communication problems, and others will have better results. JT does have a lot of knowledge, and he does care about his work ‚Äì he just didn‚Äôt seem to be open to the possibility that he had made a mistake.
As is usually the case, there are two sides to every story. I am sure that JT and his brother will have different memories of the events. I hoped that I could walk out today a happy customer and shake hands with JT and his brother for standing behind their work, but that‚Äôs not always how things work.
Good bye, JT ‚Äì have a nice day!<//review>

<Review>Dr. Cassileth and Dr. Richardson's all-female team has been my dream come true throughout the mastectomy and reconstruction process. They have laughed with me, cried with me, listened to me, held my hands, and advocated for me like I was their own family.

As a medical professional with a genetically high risk for breast cancer, I knew I would need a prophylactic mastectomy rather than face an almost certain cancer diagnosis. I did literally years of research into the multitude of methods, finding along the way horror stories about multi-stage procedures, painful tissue expanders, flap necrosis, abdominal nipple transplants, and a general lack of grace and understanding in the medical community about women's needs and health. After all this disappointing research, I found Dr. Cassileth's method online describing the optimal nipple-sparing, minimal scarring, one-stage mastectomy and reconstruction, and I knew I had to meet this team. With my very first phone call to the office, I had complete confidence in them. They were so compassionate and forthright with information about the surgery, expectations, costs, and planning over the phone. I live a 3-hour car ride away from Beverly Hills, and they were so accommodating to fit in as many pre-op tasks as possible into my consultation appointment to help reduce my travel burden. (In contrast, other offices I contacted were difficult to reach, schedulers were short with me over the phone, and minimal information was provided regarding the surgeon's methods and costs.)

During the consultation, the surgeons were able to come up with the ideal surgical plan for me using the most advanced technology and surgical methods, including a new nerve grafting method that can increase one's chance of regaining breast sensation over time (researching online showed that most other methods leave the breast numb for the rest of your life!). After my initial consultation, I was able to communicate with the team using a secure app called Klara which I found very convenient, like texting. Any time I had a question, or needed to send documents to the office, I could do so on Klara and would receive timely responses from the team. I even made my payments online.

On my surgery date, I felt no anxiety or concerns about my procedure; the team left no stone unturned regarding expectations, outcomes, and the healing process. Post-op I was left with the most overwhelming feeling of gratitude and relief knowing that cancer will no longer be my fate, and that my surgical result would look like my own, natural breasts. The team set up my post-op stay with Serenity Aftercare, making my first few nights post-op completely worry free. They took care of everything from meals and pillows to drains and catheters. The first few days, my pain was controlled with just ibuprofen and acetaminophen. I only needed the narcotic pain medicine a couple of times when I was getting in the car and would need some extra pain control.

A week following my procedure, I developed some fluid build up under one breast. I was able to send a video to the team in Klara to show them my area of concern. They made me an appointment the very next day in the office where they reassured me that this was totally normal and not at all a risk to my outcomes. For my comfort, Dr. Richardson was able to gently and safely remove the fluid from the breast. This just goes to show how responsive this team is when an issue arises, and how well they listen to their patients' concerns; even though the fluid pocket was not a risk to my health, they still understood that removing it was going to help my piece of mind and my overall healing.

I am now 10-days post-op and I feel quite independent at home. I am taking it easy, and not lifting anything heavy or over-doing my activity, but I am able to do basic cooking, get dressed by myself, etc. I have felt some muscle soreness but have never had sharp or intense pain. I can't recommend this team and this surgical method enough, and I can't thank the entire team enough for providing truly the best care!<//Review>< Pics>
